 'government is framing allies in corruption' Advani said that the BJP had launched a campaign against corruption in the winter session of Parliament last year and forced the government to set up a joint parliamentary committee in the 2G spectrum allocation case
 unhone kaha ki congress sahyogiyon ko bali kaa bakra bana kar ghotaale ke liye jimmedaar apane netaaon ko bachaa rahi he
 We have no sympathy with the allies and all corrupt people should be punished
 bhrashtachar ke khilaaf adwani ne bhari hunkaarkale dhan ke mudde par adwani ne kaha ki agar swiss bainkon main jamaa 25 lakh karod rupaya waapas aa jaae to desh ke sabhi chah lakh gaanvon kaa vikaas ho saktaa he
 He said that the British rulers looted one lakh crores rupees in 200 years of rule, while the corrupt elements took 25 lakh crores rupees in 60 years
 kendriya mantri venkaiya naidu ne madhya pradesh main simi ke aath aatankiyon ke encounter par sawaal uthaane vaale vipaksh ko hi katghare main khadaa kar diya he

 sawaal uthaane vaale pehle iskaa jawaab den

 Venkaiah Naidu also said that i appeal to the Congress party and its allies not to give it a political color because it can spoil the atmosphere of the country
 My question is only why so much sympathy with terrorists? And why so much sympathy with Simi? The judicial inquiry into the encounter will clear everything and the law will do its job
 venkaiya naidu ne yah bhi kaha ki ham congress se puche ki unhone apane samay par kya kiya
 NIA is the largest agency in the country to investigate terrorist incidents and terrorists
 kya ham aatankwaadiyon se puche unki jaat kya he dharm kya he? enie diji par sawaal nahin khadey karne chahie unka kaarykaal kin paristhitiyon main bahaya gaya he yah dekhnaa chahie
 BJP MP and former Mumbai Police Commissioner Satpal Singh said that any encounters in the country are questioned, but we should trust the police
 jinka kaa encounter kiya gaya he, wo 2013 main bhi khandwa jail se bhaage the

 saansad ne kaha kiencounterki nyaayik jaanch hogi to sab pataa chal jayega
 Their escape from jail is a mistake of the administration
 agar ye ek consteble ko markar bhaag jate to aap kehete ki police ne kuch nahin kiya, isliye police ko badhai deni chahie
 Satpal said that the government sacked the DG of the jail after running away from jail, this is a good move
 encounter par sawaal uthaane par satpal ne kaha ki pichley 15 saal main sabase zyada encounter maharashtra or mumbai main congress kii sarkaar main hue hai

 enie par sabko bharosa he, lekin ye kah rahe hai ki diji kaa kaarykaal badhaayaa gaya he, isliye jaanch nishpaksh nahin hogi

 shaan marsh (naabad 68) kii match jitau pari kii badaulat kings ilevan punjab team ne vankhede stadium main ravivaar ko khele gaye indian premier lig (ipel) ke paanchaven sanskaran ke 28wein lig mukaable main mumbai indiens ko chah wicket se haraa diya
 This is Kings xi's third win, while Mumbai Indians have got their third defeat
 marsh ko main of da match chunaa gaya
 Kings XI scored 19, chasing a 164-run challenge put on by the Mumbai Indians
 3 over kii ballebaaji main chaar wicket khokar jeet hasil kar lee
 Marsh hit five fours and three sixes in a 40-ball innings
 iske alaava salaami ballebaaj nitin saini ne 30 or mandeep singh ne 24 ran banaae
 Captain David Hussey also contributed 21 runs
 saini or mandeep ne pehle wicket ke liye 48 ran jode the
 After this, the captain and Marsh played the biggest and important partnership of 58 runs for the third wicket
 ajahar mahmud (10) ne niraash kiya lekin wicket par rahete hue unhone marsh ke saath 13 gendon par teji se 21 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 After this, Marsh and David Miller added 24 runs from 12 balls in the final two overs to give their team the victory with three balls remaining
 kings ilevan ne ab tak kul saat match khele hai
 He has won three and lost four
 uske khate main chah ank hai or vah nau tiimon kii talika main saatven sthaan par he
 On the other hand, the 2011 runners-up Mumbai Indians team could not win despite the return of Sachin Tendulkar
 usne ab tak kul chah match khele hai
 He has won in three while he has lost in as many matches
 mumbai indiens team chah ankon ke saath talika main chathe sthaan par he
 Earlier, winning the toss and batting, the hosts scored 163 for six in the allotted 20 overs
 isamen salaami ballebaaj james franklin ke sabase adhik 79 ran shaamil the
 Apart from this, Dinesh Karthik added 35 runs
 chaar maichon se team se baahar rahe sachin ne franklin ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 51 ran jode
 Sachin scored 23 runs off 23 balls with the help of three fours
 rohit sharma (2) saste main out hue lekin iske baad franklin ne karthik ke saath tisare wicket ke liye 75 ranon kii keemtee saajhedaari nibhaai
 Both added so many runs from just 36 balls
 karthik kaa wicket 131 ran ke kul yoga par gira
 Karthik hit five fours in his 20-ball innings
 iske baad keran pollard (7) kaa wicket 142 ran ke kul yoga par gira
 Franklin also lost his control after Pollard was dismissed
 unka wicket 152 ran ke kul yoga par gira
 Franklin hit six fours and four sixes in a 51-ball fast innings
 tippaniyan Franklin's wicket fell on the third ball of the 19th over
 agali hi gend par praveen kumaar ne captain harbhajan singh ko bhi out kar diya
 Harbhajan could score only four runs
 ambati raidu or thisira perera teen-teen ran par naabad laute
 Praveen and Parvinder Awana took two wickets each from Kings XI
 kings ilevan kii yah teesri jeet he jabaki mumbai indiens ko teesri haar mili he
 Marsh was voted man of the match
 mumbai indiens dwaara rakhi gai 164 ranon kii chunauti kaa peechha karte hue kings ilevan ne 19
 Won by winning four wickets in 3 overs batting
 marsh ne 40 gendon kii pari main paanch chauke or teen chakke lagaae
 Apart from this, opener Nitin Saini scored 30 and Mandeep Singh scored 24 runs
 captain david hasi ne bhi 21 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Saini and Mandeep had added 48 runs for the first wicket
 iske baad captain or marsh ne tisare wicket ke liye 58 ranon kii sabase badi or ahm saajhedaari nibhaai
 Azhar Mahmood (10) disappointed but while on the wicket, he shared a quick 21-run partnership with Marsh from 13 balls
 iske baad marsh or david miller ne antim do overon main 12 gendon par 24 ran jodakar apni team ko teen gend shesh rahete jeet dilaa di
 Kings XI have played a total of seven matches so far
 use teen main jeet or chaar main haar mili he
 He has six points on his account and is seventh in the table of nine teams
 duusari ore, 2011 kii upavijeta mumbai indiens team sachin tendulkar kii vaapasi ke baavjood jeet hasil nahin kar saki
 He has played a total of six matches so far
 teen main use jeet mili he jabaki itane hi maichon main haar mili he
 The Mumbai Indians team is sixth in the table with six points
 isse pehle, toss jitkar ballebaaji karte hue mejabaan team ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main chah wicket par 163 ran banaae
 It included opener James Franklin with 79 runs at most
 iske alaava dinesh karthik ne 35 ran jode
 Sachin, who was out of the team for four matches, added 51 runs for the first wicket with Franklin
 sachin ne 23 gendon par teen chaukon kii madad se 23 ran banaae
 Rohit Sharma (2) was dismissed cheaply but after that Franklin shared a valuable 75-run partnership for the third wicket with Karthik
 donon ne maatr 36 gendon par itane ran jode
 Karthik's wicket fell at a total of 131 runs
 karthik ne apni 20 gendon kii pari main paanch chauke lagaae
 After this, the wicket of Karen Pollard (7) fell to a total of 142 runs
 pollard ke out hone ke baad franklin bhi apana sanyam kho baithe
 His wicket fell at a total of 152 runs
 franklin ne 51 gendon kii tej pari main chah chauke or chaar chakke lagaae
 The comments franklin kaa wicket 19wein over kii teesri gend par gira
 On the next ball, Praveen Kumar also dismissed captain Harbhajan Singh
 harbhajan sirf chaar ran bana sake
 Ambati Rayudu and Thisira Perera returned unbeaten on three runs each

 charitra pramaan patr ke liye aavedan karnaa ab sirf ek clic dur he

 varsh 1999 ke vishwa cap main is trophy ko ek aadhikarik naam diya gaya, isisi vishwacap trophy
 
 
 Earlier it was known as Prudential Cup, Benson & Hedges Cup, Wills Trophy and Reliance Cup

 In 1975, when the World Cup was first played, England's life insurance company Prudential Corp decided to sponsor it, and its condition was that its name be added to the cup, so the ICC did the same
 
 
 iske baad varsh 1979 or 1983 ke vishwacap ke dauraan bhi trophy ko prudential cap ke naam se janaa gaya

 1983 main bharat ne vishwacap jeeta or is tarah yah cap pehali baar bharat aayaa
